"published-print": {"date-parts": [[2005, 11, 7]]}, "abstract": "<jats:p>Integrin-mediated cell adhesion to extracellular matrix proteins is known to promote cell survival, whereas detachment from the matrix can cause rapid apoptotic death in some cell types. Contrary to this paradigm, we show that fibroblast adhesion to the angiogenic matrix protein CCN1 (CYR61) induces apoptosis, whereas endothelial cell adhesion to CCN1 promotes cell survival. CCN1 induces fibroblast apoptosis through its adhesion receptors, integrin \u03b16\u03b21 and the heparan sulfate proteoglycan (HSPG) syndecan-4, triggering the transcription-independent p53 activation of Bax to render cytochrome c release and activation of caspase-9 and -3. Neither caspase-8 activity nor de novo transcription or translation is required for this process. These results show that cellular interaction with a specific matrix protein can either induce or suppress apoptosis in a cell type\u2013specific manner and that integrin \u03b16\u03b21-HSPGs can function as receptors to induce p53-dependent apoptosis.</jats:p>", "DOI": "10.1083/jcb.200504015", "type": "journal-article", "created": {"date-parts": [[2005, 11, 7]], "date-time": "2005-11-07T20:02:47Z", "timestamp": 1131393767000}, "page": "559-568", "update-policy": "http://dx.doi.org/10.1083/jcb.crossmarkpolicy", "source": "Crossref", "is-referenced-by-count": 76, "title": ["The matrix protein CCN1 (CYR61) induces apoptosis in fibroblasts"], "prefix": "10.1083", "volume": "171", "author": [{"given": "Viktor", "family": "Todorovicc\u0327", "sequence": "first", "affiliation": [{"name": "Department of Biochemistry and Molecular Genetics, University of Illinois at Chicago College of Medicine, Chicago, IL 60607"}]}, {"given": "Chih-Chiun", "family": "Chen", "sequence": "additional", "affiliation": [{"name": "Department of Biochemistry and Molecular Genetics, University of Illinois at Chicago College of Medicine, Chicago, IL 60607"}]}, {"given": "Nissim", "family": "Hay", "sequence": "additional", "affiliation": [{"name": "Department of Biochemistry and Molecular Genetics, University of Illinois at Chicago College of Medicine, Chicago, IL 60607"}]}, {"given": "Lester F.", "family": "Lau", "sequence": "additional", "affiliation": [{"name": "Department of Biochemistry and Molecular Genetics, University of Illinois at Chicago College of Medicine, Chicago, IL 60607"}]}], "member": "291", "published-online": {"date-parts": [[2005, 11, 7]]}, "reference": [{"key": "2019121104391042600_BIB1", "volume": "149", "first-page": "741", "year": "2000", "journal-title": "J.
